## ❆❜/a115/a116/a114❛❝/a116

❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115✳ ✹✷

❍♦✇❡✈❡/a114✱ ❛ ❧❛/a114❣❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ /a114❡/a113✉✐/a114❡❞ /a116♦ /a114❡❛❝❤ ❛ ✹✸ ❣✐✈❡♥ ❢❛❧/a115❡ ❞✐/a115❝♦✈❡/a114② /a114❛/a116❡ ✭❋❉❘✮ ❧❡✈❡❧ ♦♥ /a115♦♠❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115✳ ❆/a115 ❛♥ ❡①❛♠♣❧❡✱ ✇❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ✹✹

●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ●❡♥❡ ❖♥/a116♦❧♦❣② ❇✐♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧ /a80❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✭❈✺❴❇/a80 /a115✉❜/a115❡/a116 ♦❢ ▼❙✐❣❉❇ ✹✺ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ❬✶❪✮ ♦♥ ❢♦✉/a114 ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ ●❡♥❡ ❊①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❖♠♥✐❜✉/a115 ✭●❊❖✮ ✈❛/a114②✐♥❣ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ✹✻ ❞❡♣/a116❤✱ ❛♥❞ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 /a114❡❛❝❤✐♥❣ ❋❉❘ ❧❡✈❡❧ ♦❢ ✵✳✵✶ ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❇❡♥❥❛♠✐♥✐✲ ✹✼ ❍♦❝❤❜❡/a114❣ ✭❇❍✮ ❝♦/a114/a114❡❝/a116✐♦♥✳ ❉✉❡ /a116♦ /a116❤❡ ♣/a114♦♣❡/a114/a116✐❡/a115 ♦❢ ❇❍ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡✱ /a116❤❡ ❞❡♣❡♥❞❡♥❝❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ✹✽ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✐♥ /a116❤❡/a115❡ ❡①♣❡/a114✐♠❡♥/a116/a115 ❤❛/a115 ❛ ♣❤❛/a115❡ /a116/a114❛♥/a115✐/a116✐♦♥ ❜❡❤❛✈✐♦/a114 ✭❋✐❣ ✶❜✮✿ ✹✾ ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 /a116❤❡/a114❡ ❡①✐/a115/a116 ❛ ❝❡/a114/a116❛✐♥ ❝/a114✐/a116✐❝❛❧ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ✇❤✐❝❤ /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ✺✵ ♦❢ /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❜❡❝♦♠❡/a115 ♥♦♥✲③❡/a114♦ ❛♥❞ /a115/a116❛②/a115 ♦♥ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ ❧❡✈❡❧✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ❝/a114✐/a116✐❝❛❧ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ✺✶ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ✐/a115 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ❢♦/a114 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115✱ ❜✉/a116 ✉❧/a116✐♠❛/a116❡❧② ❝❛♥ /a114❡❛❝❤ /a116❤❡ ♦/a114❞❡/a114 ♦❢ M/α ✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ α ✺✷ ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ /a115❡❧❡❝/a116❡❞ ❋❉❘ /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞ ❛♥❞ M ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114❡❞ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115✳ ✺✸

❍♦✇❡✈❡/a114✱ ❛❝❝✉/a114❛/a116❡❧② ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♥❣ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❧♦✇❡/a114 /a116❤❛♥ 10 -5 ✇✐/a116❤ ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ✐♠♣/a114❛❝/a116✐❝❛❧ ♦/a114 ❡✈❡♥ ✐♥❢❡❛/a115✐❜❧❡✳ ❚♦ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡ /a115✉❝❤ ❧♦✇ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇❡ ❞❡✈❡❧♦♣❡❞ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞✱ ✇❤✐❝❤ ✐/a115 ❜❛/a115❡❞ ♦♥ ❛♥ ❛❞❛♣/a116✐✈❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115♣❧✐/a116 ▼♦♥/a116❡ ❈❛/a114❧♦ /a115❝❤❡♠❡ ❬✻❪✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ /a116❛❦❡/a115 ❛/a115 ❛♥ ✐♥♣✉/a116 ❛♥ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡ γ &gt; 0 ❛♥❞ ❛ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a115✐③❡ K ✱ ❛♥❞ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ♣/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② P K (ES glyph[greaterorequalslant] γ ) ♦❢ ❛ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K /a116♦ ❤❛✈❡ ❛♥ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ γ ✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ /a115❡/a113✉❡♥/a116✐❛❧❧② ✜♥❞/a115 ❊❙ ❧❡✈❡❧/a115 l i ❢♦/a114 ✇❤✐❝❤ /a116❤❡ ♣/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② P K (ES glyph[greaterorequalslant] l i ) ✐/a115 ❛♣♣/a114♦①✐♠❛/a116❡❧② ❡/a113✉❛❧ /a116♦ 2 -i ✭/a115❡❡ ❋✐❣ ✸❛ ❢♦/a114 ❛ /a116♦② ❡①❛♠♣❧❡✮✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ /a115/a116♦♣/a115 ✇❤❡♥ l i ❜❡❝♦♠❡/a115 ❣/a114❡❛/a116❡/a114 /a116❤❛♥ γ ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ❝/a114✉❞❡❧② ❛♣♣/a114♦①✐♠❛/a116❡❞ ❛/a115 2 -i ✳

❚❤❡ ✐♥/a116❡/a114♠❡❞✐❛/a116❡ l i /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❛/a115 ❢♦❧❧♦✇/a115✳ ❋✐/a114/a115/a116✱ ❛ /a115❡/a116 ♦❢ Z ✭❛♥ ♦❞❞ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114✱ ♣❛/a114❛♠❡/a116❡/a114 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞✮ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K ❛/a114❡ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ ✉♥✐❢♦/a114♠❧② ❛♥❞ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡♠ ❛/a114❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡❞✐❛♥ ✈❛❧✉❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✐/a115 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❛♥❞ ❛/a115/a115✐❣♥❡❞ /a116♦ l 1 ✳ ❇② ❝♦♥/a115/a116/a114✉❝/a116✐♦♥✱ /a116❤❡ ♣/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② P K ( γ glyph[greaterorequalslant] l 1 ) ♦❢ ❛ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a116♦ ❤❛✈❡ ❛♥ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡ ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ l 1 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ❛♣♣/a114♦①✐♠❛/a116❡❞ ❛/a115 1 2 ✳ ◆❡①/a116 Z -1 2 ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥

l 1 ❛/a114❡ ❞✐/a115❝❛/a114❞❡❞✱ ✇❤✐❧❡ Z -1 2 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❣/a114❡❛/a116❡/a114 /a116❤❛♥ l 1 ❛/a114❡ ❞✉♣❧✐❝❛/a116❡❞✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ✶✷✸ /a114❡/a115✉❧/a116/a115 ✐♥ ❛ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ ♦❢ Z ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ l 1 ✱ ❜✉/a116 /a116❤❡ ❞✐/a115/a116/a114✐❜✉/a116✐♦♥ ✐/a115 ✶✷✹ ♥♦♥✲✉♥✐❢♦/a114♠✳ ❍♦✇❡✈❡/a114✱ ✐/a116 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ♠❛❞❡ ✐♥/a116♦ ❛ ✉♥✐❢♦/a114♠ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ ✇✐/a116❤ ❛ ▼❡/a116/a114♦♣♦❧✐/a115 ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠✳ ✶✷✺ ❖♥ ❡❛❝❤ ▼❡/a116/a114♦♣♦❧✐/a115 ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ /a115/a116❡♣ ❡❛❝❤ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a115❛♠♣❧❡ ✐/a115 /a116/a114✐❡❞ /a116♦ ❜❡ ♠♦❞✐✜❡❞ ❜② /a115✇❛♣♣✐♥❣ ✶✷✻ ❛ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ ❢/a114♦♠ /a116❤❡ /a115❡/a116 ✇✐/a116❤ ❛ ❣❡♥❡ ♦✉/a116/a115✐❞❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a115❡/a116✳ ❚❤❡ ❝❤❛♥❣❡ ✐/a115 ❛❝❝❡♣/a116❡❞ ✐❢ ❛♥ ✶✷✼ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ♥❡✇ /a115❡/a116 ✐/a115 ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❡♥ ❝✉/a114/a114❡♥/a116 /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞ l 1 ✱ ♦/a116❤❡/a114✇✐/a115❡ /a116❤❡ ❝❤❛♥❣❡ ✐/a115 ✶✷✽ /a114❡❥❡❝/a116❡❞✳ ▼❡/a116/a114♦♣♦❧✐/a115 ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❣✉❛/a114❛♥/a116❡❡/a115✱ /a116❤❛/a116 ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❡♥♦✉❣❤ /a115/a116❡♣/a115 /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ ❜❡❝♦♠❡/a115 ❝❧♦/a115❡ ✶✷✾ /a116♦ ✉♥✐❢♦/a114♠❧② ❞✐/a115/a116/a114✐❜✉/a116❡❞✳ ❚❤✉/a115✱ ❛ ♠❡❞✐❛♥ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 ✭ l 2 ✮ ✇♦✉❧❞ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞ /a116♦ ✶✸✵ ♣/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② ♦❢ 1 2 ❢♦/a114 ❛ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a116♦ ❤❛✈❡ ❛♥ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ l 2 ❣✐✈❡♥ ✐/a116 ❤❛/a115 ❛♥ ✶✸✶ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ♥♦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ l 1 ✿ ✶✸✷

❚❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✐/a115 ❛♣♣❧✐❡❞ /a116♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ /a116❤❡ ♥❡①/a116 l i ✈❛❧✉❡/a115✳ ✶✸✹

❲❤❡♥ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♥❣ /a115♠❛❧❧ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✐/a116 ❜❡❝♦♠❡/a115 ♣/a114❛❝/a116✐❝❛❧ /a116♦ ❝❛/a114/a114② ♦✉/a116 /a116❤❡ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥ ✐♥ ❧♦❣✲ ✶✸✼ /a115❝❛❧❡✳ ■♥ ♣❛/a114/a116✐❝✉❧❛/a114✱ /a116❤❡ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❜❡❝♦♠❡ ♣/a114❛❝/a116✐❝❛❧❧② ✉♥❜✐❛/a115❡❞ ❜♦/a116❤ ✐♥ ♠❡❞✐❛♥ ❛♥❞ ♠❡❛♥ /a115❡♥/a115❡ ✶✸✽ ❛♥❞ ✐/a116 ❜❡❝♦♠❡/a115 /a115✐♠♣❧❡ /a116♦ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡ /a116❤❡ ❛♣♣/a114♦①✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥ ❡/a114/a114♦/a114 ❛♥❞ ❝♦♥❞✐❢❡♥❝❡ ✐♥/a116❡/a114✈❛❧/a115 ✭/a115❡❡ ✶✸✾ /a115❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✷✳✺✳✹✮✳ ✶✹✵

❚❤❡ ❢✉❧❧ ❢♦/a114♠❛❧ ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐♣/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✐/a115 ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ✐♥ /a116❤❡ /a115❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✷✳✺✳ ✶✹✶

❚♦ ❢✉/a114/a116❤❡/a114 ♣/a114♦✈❡ /a116❤❡ ❛♣♣/a114♦①✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥ /a113✉❛❧✐/a116② ♦❢ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✇❡ ❞❡✈❡❧♦♣❡❞ ❛♥ ❡①❛❝/a116 ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❢♦/a114 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♥❣ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115✱ ❜✉/a116 ❧✐♠✐/a116❡❞ /a116♦ ✐♥/a116❡❣❡/a114 ✇❡✐❣❤/a116/a115✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ✐/a115 ❜❛/a115❡❞ ♦♥ ❞②♥❛♠✐❝ ♣/a114♦❣/a114❛♠♠✐♥❣✱ /a116❤❡ ❢✉❧❧ ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐♣/a116✐♦♥ ✐/a115 ❣✐✈❡♥ ✐♥ /a115❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✷✳✹✳ ❚❤❡ ❝♦♠♣❧❡①✐/a116② ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✐/a115 O ( NKT 2 ) ✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ N ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡/a115✱ K ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ /a115✐③❡ ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ❛♥❞ T ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ /a115✉♠ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a116♦♣ K ❛❜/a115♦❧✉/a116❡ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝/a115✳ ❲✐/a116❤ ❛ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ♦♣/a116✐♠✐③❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 /a116❤✐/a115 ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❛❧❧♦✇/a115 /a116♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a114♦✉♥❞❡❞ ✇❡✐❣❤/a116/a115 ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ❡①❛♠♣❧❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116 ✐♥ ❛ ❝♦✉♣❧❡ ♦❢ ❤♦✉/a114/a115✳

■♥ ♣/a114❛❝/a116✐❝❡ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ✐/a115 ❝♦♠❜✐♥❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡✳ ❋✐/a114/a115/a116✱ ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡ ✐♥♣✉/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❝❛♥ ❜❡ /a114✉♥ ✇✐/a116❤ ❛ ❧✐♠✐/a116❡❞ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡✳ ◆❡①/a116✱ ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 /a116❤❛/a116 ❤❛✈❡ ❤✐❣❤ /a114❡❧❛/a116✐✈❡ ❡/a114/a114♦/a114 ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ✭✐✳❡✳ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ ❧♦✇ ♣✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115✮ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ✐/a115 ❡①❡❝✉/a116❡❞✳ ❆/a115 ♠❛♥② ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✐♥ ❛♥ ✐♥♣✉/a116 ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✉/a115✉❛❧❧② ❛/a114❡ ♥♦/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤❡❞✱ /a116❤❡② ❤❛✈❡ ❛ /a114❡❧❛/a116✐✈❡❧② ❤✐❣❤ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❛♥❞ ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ❜❛/a116❝❤✲♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ ❛ ❤✐❣❤❧② ❡✣❝✐❡♥/a116 ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✇✐/a116❤ ❞❡/a116❡/a114♠✐♥✐/a115/a116✐❝ /a116✐♠❡ ❜♦✉♥❞❛/a114✐❡/a115✳ ❚❤❡ ♠♦/a114❡ ✐♥/a116❡/a114❡/a115/a116✐♥❣ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ ❧♦✇❡/a114 /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇✐❧❧ /a116❤❡♥ ❜❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✐♥❞✐✈✐❞✉❛❧❧② ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ ❛♠♦✉♥/a116 ♦❢ ♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115✐♥❣ /a116✐♠❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❞❡♣❡♥❞ ♦♥ /a116❤❡✐/a114 /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115✳

❋✐♥❛❧❧②✱ ✇❡ ❤❛✈❡ ❡①♣❧♦/a114❡❞ ❋●❙❊❆ ♣❡/a114❢♦/a114♠❛♥❝❡ ♦♥ /a116❤❡ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ✻✵✺ ❝✉/a114❛/a116❡❞ ●❊❖ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐❜❡❞ ❡❛/a114❧✐❡/a114 ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ ❈✺❴❇/a80 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥✳ ◆♦/a116❛❜❧②✱ ✐/a116 /a116♦♦❦ ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❡♥ ❛ ♠✐♥✉/a116❡ ♣❡/a114 ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116 ♦❢ /a114✉♥♥✐♥❣ /a116✐♠❡ /a116♦ ✜♥✐/a115❤ ❋●❙❊❆ ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✭❋✐❣ ✹❛✮ ♦♥ ❛ ❧❛♣/a116♦♣ ✇✐/a116❤ ✹✲❝♦/a114❡ ■♥/a116❡❧ ❈♦/a114❡ ✐✺ ♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115♦/a114✱ ✇✐/a116❤ ❛ ♠❡❞✐❛♥ /a116✐♠❡ ♦❢ ✽ /a115❡❝♦♥❞/a115✳ ❇❡/a115✐❞❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠✱ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ✇❛/a115 ❝❛/a114/a114✐❡❞ ♦✉/a116 ✇✐/a116❤ ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ♦❢ n = 10 3 ✱ 10 4 ❛♥❞ 10 5 ✱ ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ /a114❡❢❡/a114❡♥❝❡ ✐♠♣❧❡✲ ♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ ✭❇/a114♦❛❞ ●❙❊❆✮ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ♦❢ 10 4 ✳ ❋♦/a114 ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡/a115❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞/a115 ✇❡ ❝♦♠♣❛/a114❡❞ /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 /a114❡❛❝❤✐♥❣ ❋❉❘ ❧❡✈❡❧ ♦❢ ✵✳✵✶✿ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ ✉/a115❡❞ ❢♦/a114 ❋●❙❊❆ ❛♥❞ /a114❡♣♦/a114/a116❡❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✭ ❇/a114♦❛❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✮ ✇❡/a114❡ ✉/a115❡❞ ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ /a114❡❢❡/a114❡♥❝❡ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ ✭❋✐❣ ✹❜✮✳ ❚❤❡ /a114❡/a115✉❧/a116/a115 /a114❡✐/a116❡/a114❛/a116❡ /a116❤❛/a116 ❡✈❡♥ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ♦❢ 10 5 ✐/a115 ♥♦/a116 ❡♥♦✉❣❤ /a116♦ ❞❡/a116❡❝/a116 /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115✲ /a116✐❝❛❧❧② /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤❡❞ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a115♦♠❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ✇❤❡♥ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116♠❡♥/a116 ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✐/a115 ✉/a115❡❞✳

❚❤❡ ❛❞ ❤♦❝ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❡❞ ✐♥ ❇/a114♦❛❞ ●❙❊❆ ❛❣❣/a114❡❣❛/a116❡/a115 ❊❙ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❛❝/a114♦/a115/a115 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✐♥❝/a114❡❛/a115✐♥❣ /a116❤❡ /a115❡♥/a115✐/a116✐✈✐/a116② ♦♥ /a115♦♠❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ❝♦♠♣❛/a114❡❞ /a116♦ ❇❍✲

❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ♦❢ 10 4 ✱ ❤♦✇❡✈❡/a114 /a116❤✐/a115 ✐♥❝/a114❡❛/a115❡ ✐♥ /a115❡♥/a115✐/a116✐✈✐/a116② ❝♦♠❡/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ ♦✈❡/a114❛❧❧ ♠♦/a114❡ ❝♦♥/a115❡/a114✈❛/a116✐✈❡ ❜❡❤❛✈✐♦/a114✳ ❚❤❡ /a116♦/a116❛❧ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 /a114❡❛❝❤✐♥❣ ❋❉❘ ❧❡✈❡❧ ♦❢ ✵✳✵✶ ❢♦/a114 ❇/a114♦❛❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✐/a115 ✸✾✹✻✼✱ ✇❤✐❝❤ ✐/a115 ♦♥❧② ✻✵✪ ♦❢ ✻✺✻✾✵ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116♠❡♥/a116 /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ♦❢ 10 4 ❛♥❞ ✹✽✪ ♦❢ ✽✶✻✷✽ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠✳ ❲❡ ❢✉/a114/a116❤❡/a114 ❝❤❛/a114❛❝/a116❡/a114✐③❡❞ /a116❤✐/a115 ❜❡❤❛✈✐♦/a114 ❜② ❞✐/a114❡❝/a116❧② ❝♦♠♣❛/a114✐♥❣ ❇/a114♦❛❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛♥❞ ❤❛✈❡ /a115❤♦✇♥ /a116❤❛/a116 ❇/a114♦❛❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a114❡ ✐♥❞✐✈✐❞✉❛❧❧② ♠♦/a114❡ ❝♦♥/a115❡/a114✈❛/a116✐✈❡ ✭❋✐❣ ✹❝✮ ✐♥ ❛ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② /a115✐③❡ ❞❡♣❡♥❞❡♥/a116 ♠❛♥♥❡/a114 ✭❋✐❣ ✹❞✮✳

❚♦ ❝♦♥❝❧✉❞❡✱ ❤❡/a114❡ ✇❡ ❤❛✈❡ ♣/a114❡/a115❡♥/a116❡❞ ❋●❙❊❆ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❢♦/a114 ❢❛/a115/a116 ♣/a114❡/a114❛♥❦❡❞ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤✲ ♠❡♥/a116 ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115✳ ❚❤❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❛❧❧♦✇/a115 /a116♦ /a114♦✉/a116✐♥❡❧② ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡ ❡✈❡♥ ✈❡/a114② ❧♦✇ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛♥❞ ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ✉/a115❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ ❝♦♥❥✉♥❝/a116✐♦♥ ✇✐/a116❤ /a115/a116❛♥❞❛/a114❞ ♠✉❧/a116✐♣❧❡ ❤②♣♦/a116❤❡/a115✐/a115 /a116❡/a115/a116✐♥❣ ❝♦/a114/a114❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞/a115✱ /a115✉❝❤ ❛/a115 ❇❡♥❥❛♠✐♥✐✲❍♦❝❤❜❡/a114❣ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡✳ ❚❤✐/a115✱ ✐♥ /a116✉/a114♥✱ ❧❡❛❞/a115 /a116♦ ❜❡/a116/a116❡/a114 /a115❡♥/a115✐/a116✐✈✐/a116② ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ ❛❜✐❧✐/a116② /a116♦ ❞❡/a116❡❝/a116 /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✐♥ ❤❛/a114❞ ❝❛/a115❡/a115✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ ♦/a116❤❡/a114 ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ❢❛✐❧✳ ❋●❙❊❆ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ✐/a115 ❢/a114❡❡❧② ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ❛/a115 ❛♥ ❘ ♣❛❝❦❛❣❡ ❛/a116 ❇✐♦❝♦♥❞✉❝/a116♦/a114 ✭❤/a116/a116♣✿✴✴❜✐♦❝♦♥❞✉❝/a116♦/a114✳♦/a114❣✴♣❛❝❦❛❣❡/a115✴❢❣/a115❡❛✮ ❛♥❞ ♦♥ ●✐/a116❍✉❜ ✭❤/a116/a116♣/a115✿✴✴❣✐/a116❤✉❜✳❝♦♠✴❝/a116❧❛❜✴❢❣/a115❡❛✮✳

❚❤❡ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ❛/a114/a114❛② S ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a115✐③❡ | S | = N ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ❣❡♥❡ i ∈ U ❝♦♥/a116❛✐♥/a115 ❛ ✈❛❧✉❡ S i ∈ R /a116❤❛/a116 ❝❤❛/a114❛❝/a116❡/a114✐③❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡ ❜❡❤❛✈✐♦/a114 ✐♥ ❛ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114❡❞ ❜✐♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧ ♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115✳ ❈♦♠♠♦♥❧②✱ ✐❢ S i &gt; 0 /a116❤❡ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡ i ❣♦❡/a115 ✉♣ ♦♥ /a116/a114❡❛/a116♠❡♥/a116 ❝♦♠♣❛/a114❡❞ /a116♦ ❝♦♥/a116/a114♦❧ ❛♥❞ S i &lt; 0 ♠❡❛♥/a115 /a116❤❛/a116 /a116❤❡ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❣♦❡/a115 ❞♦✇♥✳ ❆❜/a115♦❧✉/a116❡ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 | S i | /a114❡♣/a114❡/a115❡♥/a116 ♠❛❣♥✐/a116✉❞❡ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❝❤❛♥❣❡✳ ❆/a114/a114❛② S ✐/a115 /a115♦/a114/a116❡❞ ✐♥ ❛ ❞❡❝/a114❡❛/a115✐♥❣ ♦/a114❞❡/a114✿ S i &gt; S j ❢♦/a114 i &lt; j ✳ ❚❤❡ ✈❛❧✉❡ ♦❢ N ✐♥ ♣/a114❛❝/a116✐❝❡ ✐/a115 ❛❜♦✉/a116 ✶✵✵✵✵✕✷✵✵✵✵✳

❚❤❡ ❧✐/a115/a116 ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 P = { P 1 , P 2 , . . . , P M } ♦❢ ❧❡♥❣/a116❤ M ✉/a115✉❛❧❧② ❝♦♥/a116❛✐♥/a115 ❣/a114♦✉♣/a115 ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡/a115 /a116❤❛/a116 ❛/a114❡ ❝♦♠♠♦♥❧② /a114❡❣✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ✐♥ /a115♦♠❡ ❜✐♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧ ♣/a114♦❝❡/a115/a115✳ ❲❡ ❛/a115/a115✉♠❡ /a116❤❛/a116 /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 P i ❛/a114❡ ♦/a114❞❡/a114❡❞ ❜② /a116❤❡✐/a114 /a115✐③❡ ✭❞❡♥♦/a116❡❞ ❛/a115 K i ✮✿ K 1 glyph[lessorequalslant] K 2 glyph[lessorequalslant] . . . glyph[lessorequalslant] K M = K ✳ ❯/a115✉❛❧❧② ♦♥❧② /a114❡❧❛/a116✐✈❡❧② /a115♠❛❧❧ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ K ≈ 500 ❣❡♥❡/a115✳

❚♦ /a113✉❛♥/a116✐❢② ❛ ❝♦✲/a114❡❣✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ✐♥ ❛ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 p ❙✉❜/a114❛♠❛♥✐❛♥ ❡/a116 ❛❧ ✳❬✶❪ ✐♥/a116/a114♦❞✉❝❡❞ ❛ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ❢✉♥❝/a116✐♦♥ s r ( p ) /a116❤❛/a116 ✉/a115❡/a115 ❣❡♥❡ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣/a115 ✭✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ♦❢ S ✮✳ ❚❤❡ ♠♦/a114❡ ♣♦/a115✐/a116✐✈❡ ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ ✈❛❧✉❡ ♦❢ s r ( p ) /a116❤❡ ♠♦/a114❡ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤❡❞ /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ✐/a115 ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ♣♦/a115✐/a116✐✈❡❧②✲/a114❡❣✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ✭✇✐/a116❤ S i &gt; 0 ✮✳ ❆❝❝♦/a114❞✐♥❣❧②✱ ♥❡❣❛/a116✐✈❡ s r ( p ) ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞/a115 /a116♦ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ♥❡❣❛/a116✐✈❡❧② /a114❡❣✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❣❡♥❡/a115✳

## ✷✳✷ ❚❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115

❆ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ✻✵✺ ❝✉/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ✇❛/a115 ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❢/a114♦♠ ❛ /a115❡/a116 ♦❢ ❛❧❧ ❝✉/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ✭●❉❙✮ ✐♥ ●❡♥❡ ❊①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❖♠♥✐❜✉/a115✳ ❖♥❧② /a116❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116 ✇♦ ❜✐♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧ ❝♦♥❞✐/a116✐♦♥/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ ❦❡♣/a116✳ ❉✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ✇❛/a115 ❞♦♥❡ ✉/a115✐♥❣ ❧✐♠♠❛✳ ❚❤❡ ♠♦❞❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ /a116✲/a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ✇❛/a115 ✉/a115❡❞ ❢♦/a114 ❣❡♥❡ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣✳ ❖♥❧② /a116♦♣ ✶✵✵✵✵ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❜② ❛✈❡/a114❛❣❡ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ✇❡/a114❡ ✉/a115❡❞ ✐♥ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣✳ ❚❤❡ ✜♥❛❧ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ❛/a116 ❤/a116/a116♣/a115✿✴✴❝/a116❧❛❜✳✐/a116♠♦✳/a114✉✴✜❧❡/a115✴/a115♦❢/a116✇❛/a114❡✴❢❣/a115❡❛✴❣❡♦❴/a114❛♥❦/a115✴✳

/a80❛/a116❤✇❛② ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥/a115 ❈✷❴❘❊❆❈❚❖▼❊✱ ❈✺❴❇/a80✱ ❈✷✱ ❈✺✱ ▼❙✐❣❉❇ ✇❡/a114❡ ♦❜/a116❛✐♥❡❞ ✈✐❛ ♠/a115✐❣❞❜/a114 ♣❛❝❦❛❣❡✳ ▲■◆❈❙ ♣❡/a114/a116✉/a114❜❛/a116✐♦♥ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✇❛/a115 ❞♦✇♥❧♦❛❞❡❞ ❢/a114♦♠ ❊♥/a114✐❝❤/a114 ✇❡❜✲/a115✐/a116❡✳ ❚❤❡ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞✐♥❣ ❣♠/a116 ✜❧❡/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ❛/a116 ❤/a116/a116♣/a115✿✴✴❝/a116❧❛❜✳✐/a116♠♦✳/a114✉✴✜❧❡/a115✴/a115♦❢/a116✇❛/a114❡✴❢❣/a115❡❛✴❣♠/a116/a115✴✳

❆/a115 /a116❤❡ ❡①❛♠♣❧❡ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣ ❚❤✵ ✈/a115 ❚❤✶ ❝♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ✇❛/a115 ✉/a115❡❞ ❢/a114♦♠ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116 ●❙❊✶✹✸✵✽ ❬✹❪✳ ❚❤❡ ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ✇❛/a115 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ✉/a115✐♥❣ ❧✐♠♠❛ ❬✽❪✳ ❖♥❧② /a116♦♣ ✶✷✵✵✵ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❜② ♠❡❛♥ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ✇❡/a114❡ ✉/a115❡❞✳ ▲✐♠♠❛ /a116✲/a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ✇❛/a115 ✉/a115❡❞ ❛/a115 ❣❡♥❡✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝✳ ❚❤❡ /a115❝/a114✐♣/a116 /a116♦ ❣❡♥✲ ❡/a114❛/a116❡ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣/a115 ✐/a115 ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ♦♥ ●✐/a116❍✉❜✿ ❤/a116/a116♣/a115✿✴✴❣✐/a116❤✉❜✳❝♦♠✴❝/a116❧❛❜✴❢❣/a115❡❛✴❜❧♦❜✴♠❛/a115/a116❡/a114✴✐♥/a115/a116✴ ❣❡♥❴❣❡♥❡❴/a114❛♥❦/a115✳❘✳

❘❡❛❝/a116♦♠❡ ❬✺❪ ❞❛/a116❛❜❛/a115❡ ✇❛/a115 ✉/a115❡❞ ❛/a115 ❛♥ ❡①❛♠♣❧❡ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✈✐❛ /a114❡❛❝/a116♦♠❡✳❞❜ ❘ ♣❛❝❦❛❣❡✳ ❋♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ♦♥❧② /a116❤❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a115✐③❡ ❢/a114♦♠ ✶✺ /a116♦ ✺✵✵ ✇❡/a114❡ ✉/a115❡❞✳ ❚❤❡ /a115❝/a114✐♣/a116 /a116♦ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✐/a115 ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ♦♥ ●✐/a116❍✉❜✿ ❤/a116/a116♣/a115✿✴✴❣✐/a116❤✉❜✳❝♦♠✴❝/a116❧❛❜✴❢❣/a115❡❛✴❜❧♦❜✴ ♠❛/a115/a116❡/a114✴✐♥/a115/a116✴❣❡♥❡❴/a114❡❛❝/a116♦♠❡❴♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115✳❘

## ✷✳✸ ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡✿ ❛♥ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❢♦/a114 ❢❛/a115/a116 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 /a115✐♠✉❧/a116❛♥❡♦✉/a115❧② ❢♦/a114 ♠❛♥② ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115

■♥ /a116❤✐/a115 /a115❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✇❡ ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐❜❡ ❛♥ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❢♦/a114 ❢❛/a115/a116 ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 /a115✐♠✉❧/a116❛♥❡♦✉/a115❧② ✷✻✵ ❢♦/a114 ❛ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 P ✳ ❚❤❡/a114❡✱ ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② p ❛ /a115❡/a116 ♦❢ n ✉♥✐❢♦/a114♠❧② /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ ✷✻✶

## ✷✳✸✳✶ ❈✉♠✉❧❛/a116✐✈❡ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ♠❡❛♥ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ✷✻✽

■♥/a115/a116❡❛❞ ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116✐♥❣ nM ✐♥❞❡♣❡♥❞❡♥/a116 /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115✿ n ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ♦❢ M ✐♥♣✉/a116 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115✱ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡ ♦♥❧② n /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K ✳ ▲❡/a116 π i ❜❡ ❛♥ i ✲/a116❤ /a114❛♥❞♦♠ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K ✳ ❋/a114♦♠ /a116❤❛/a116 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ✇❡ ❝❛♥ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛ ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡ /a113✉❡/a114② ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 P j ❜② ✉/a115✐♥❣ ✐/a116/a115 ♣/a114❡✜①✿ π i,j = π i [1 ..K j ] ✳

❚❤❡ ♥❡①/a116 /a115/a116❡♣ ✐/a115 /a116♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ /a116❤❡ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116/a115 π i,j ✳ ■♥/a115/a116❡❛❞ ♦❢ ✷✼✽

❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♥❣ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 /a115❡♣❛/a114❛/a116❡❧② ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ /a115✐♠✉❧/a116❛♥❡♦✉/a115❧② ✷✼✾ /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ π i,j ❢♦/a114 ❛ ✜①❡❞ i ✳ ❯/a115✐♥❣ ❛ /a115✐♠♣❧❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✐/a116 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ❞♦♥❡ ✐♥ Θ( K ) /a116✐♠❡✳ ✷✽✵

▲❡/a116 ✉/a115 ✜♥❞ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ ♣/a114❡✜①❡/a115 ♦❢ π i ✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ❞♦♥❡ ❜② ❡❧❡♠❡♥/a116✲✇✐/a115❡ ✷✽✶ ❞✐✈✐❞✐♥❣ ♦❢ ❝✉♠✉❧❛/a116✐✈❡ /a115✉♠/a115 ❛/a114/a114❛② ❜② /a116❤❡ ❧❡♥❣/a116❤ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞✐♥❣ ♣/a114❡✜①✿ ✷✽✷

❙❡❧❡❝/a116✐♥❣ ♦♥❧② /a116❤❡ /a114❡/a113✉✐/a114❡❞ ♣/a114❡✜①❡/a115 /a116❛❦❡/a115 ❛♥ ❛❞❞✐/a116✐♦♥❛❧ Θ( m ) /a116✐♠❡✳ ✷✽✸

## ✷✳✸✳✷ ❈✉♠✉❧❛/a116✐✈❡ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ❢♦/a114 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡

◆❡①/a116✱ ✇❡ /a115❤♦✇ ❤♦✇ /a116♦ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ✐♥ ❜❧♦❝❦/a115 ✐♥ ❛♠♦/a114/a116✐③❡❞ /a116✐♠❡ O ( b ) ✳ ❚❤✐/a115 /a116❛❦❡♥ /a116♦❣❡/a116❤❡/a114 ✇✐/a116❤ ♦♥❡ O ( b ) ♣❛/a115/a115 ✇✐❧❧ ❣❡/a116 ✉/a115 ❛♥ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ /a116♦ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ /a116❤❡ ❣❧♦❜❛❧❧② ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116 ✐♥ ❛♠♦/a114/a116✐③❡❞ O ( b ) /a116✐♠❡✳

❇❡❧♦✇ ✇❡ ✉/a115❡ c = glyph[floorleft] r k /b glyph[floorright] ❛/a115 ❛♥ ✐♥❞❡① ♦❢ ❛ ❜❧♦❝❦ ✇❤❡/a114❡ ❣❡♥❡ π k ❜❡❧♦♥❣/a115✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ r k ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ /a114❛♥❦✐♥❣ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ π ✱ ✐✳❡✳ r o i = i ✳

❋✐/a114/a115/a116✱ ✇❡ ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐❜❡ /a116❤❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ /a116♦ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ ♣♦✐♥/a116 ❝♦♦/a114❞✐♥❛/a116❡/a115✳ ❲❡ ✇✐❧❧ /a115/a116♦/a114❡ x i ❝♦♦/a114❞✐♥❛/a116❡/a115 ✉/a115✐♥❣ /a116 ✇♦ ✈❡❝/a116♦/a114/a115✿ B ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ b ❛♥❞ D ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K +1 ✱ /a115✉❝❤ /a116❤❛/a116 x i = B i/b + D i ✳ ❲❤❡♥ ❣❡♥❡ π k ✐/a115 ❛❞❞❡❞ ❛❧❧ x i ❢♦/a114 i glyph[greaterorequalslant] r k ❛/a114❡ ❞❡❝/a114❡♠❡♥/a116❡❞ ❜② ♦♥❡✳ ❚♦ /a114❡✢❡❝/a116 /a116❤✐/a115 ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❞❡❝/a114❡♠❡♥/a116 ❛❧❧ B j ❢♦/a114 j &gt; c ❛♥❞ ❞❡❝/a114❡♠❡♥/a116 ❛❧❧ D i ❢♦/a114 r k glyph[lessorequalslant] i &lt; cb ✳ ❚❤❡ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ /a116❛❦❡/a115 O ( b ) /a116✐♠❡✳ ❆❢/a116❡/a114 /a116❤✐/a115 ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✇❡ ❝❛♥ ❣❡/a116 ✈❛❧✉❡ x i ✐♥ O (1) /a116✐♠❡✳ ❚❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡ ✐/a115 ❛♣♣❧✐❡❞ ❢♦/a114 y ❝♦♦/a114❞✐♥❛/a116❡/a115✳

❙❡❝♦♥❞✱ ❢♦/a114 ❡❛❝❤ ❜❧♦❝❦ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ♠❛✐♥/a116❛✐♥ ❛♥ ✉♣♣❡/a114 ♣❛/a114/a116 ♦❢ ✐/a116/a115 ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧✳ ❍❛✈✐♥❣ ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧ ✐/a115 ✉/a115❡❢✉❧ ❜❡❝❛✉/a115❡ /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116 ✐♥ ❜❧♦❝❦ ❛❧✇❛②/a115 ❧❛②/a115 ♦♥ ✐/a116/a115 ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧✳ ❆❧❧ ❜❧♦❝❦/a115 ❡①❝❡♣/a116 c ❤❛✈❡ /a116❤❡ ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ❡✐/a116❤❡/a114 ♥♦/a116 ❝❤❛♥❣❡❞ ♦/a114 /a115❤✐❢/a116❡❞ /a115✐♠✉❧/a116❛♥❡♦✉/a115❧② ♦♥ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠❡ ✈❛❧✉❡✳ ❚❤❛/a116 ♠❡❛♥/a115 /a116❤❛/a116 /a116❤❡ ❧✐/a115/a116/a115 ♦❢ ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ♦♥ /a116❤❡ ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧/a115 ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡/a115❡ ❜❧♦❝❦/a115 /a114❡♠❛✐♥ ✉♥❝❤❛♥❣❡❞✳ ❋♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ❜❧♦❝❦ c ✇❡ ❝❛♥ /a114❡❝♦♥/a115/a116/a114✉❝/a116 ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧ ❢/a114♦♠ /a115❝/a114❛/a116❝❤ ✉/a115✐♥❣ ●/a114❛❤❛♠ /a115❝❛♥ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❬✶✵❪✳

❚♦ /a115❤♦✇ /a116❤❛/a116 /a116❤❡ ✉♣❞❛/a116✐♥❣ /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 /a116❛❦❡/a115 O ( b ) ❛♠♦/a114/a116✐③❡❞ /a116✐♠❡ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ✉/a115❡ ♣♦/a116❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞✳ ▲❡/a116 ❛ ♣♦/a116❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❛❞❞✐♥❣ k ✲/a116❤ ❣❡♥❡ Φ k ❜❡ ❛ /a115✉♠ ♦❢ /a114❡❧❛/a116✐✈❡ ✐♥❞❡①❡/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡ ❜❧♦❝❦/a115✳ ❆/a115 /a116❤❡/a114❡ ❛/a114❡ b ❜❧♦❝❦/a115 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ b /a116❤❡ /a115✉♠ ♦❢ /a114❡❧❛/a116✐✈❡ ✐♥❞❡①❡/a115 ❧✐❡/a115 ❜❡/a116✇❡❡♥ ✵ ❛♥❞ b 2 ✳ ❚❤✉/a115✱ Φ k = O ( b 2 ) ✳ ❋♦/a114 ❛♥ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡ ♦❢ ❛❧❧ b -1 ❜❧♦❝❦/a115 ❡①❝❡♣/a116 c ✇❡ ♥❡❡❞ /a116♦ ♠❛❦❡ t k = b -1 + z ♦♣❡/a114❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ♦❢ ❝♦♠♣❛/a114✐♥❣ /a116✇♦ ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ z ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ /a116✐♠❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡❞✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ❝❛♥ /a116❛❦❡ ✉♣ /a116♦ Θ( b 2 ) /a116✐♠❡ ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ✇♦/a114/a115/a116 ❝❛/a115❡✳ ❍♦✇❡✈❡/a114✱ ✐/a116 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ♥♦/a116✐❝❡❞✱ /a116❤❛/a116 ♣♦/a116❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ❝❤❛♥❣❡ Φ k -Φ k -1 ✐/a115 ❡/a113✉❛❧ /a116♦ -z + O ( b ) ✿ /a116❤❡ /a115✉♠ ♦❢ ✐♥❞❡①❡/a115 ✐/a115 ❞❡❝/a114❡❛/a115❡❞ ❜② ❛ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ /a116✐♠❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ ✉♣❞❛/a116❡❞ ♣❧✉/a115 O ( b ) ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ❜❧♦❝❦ c ✇❤❡/a114❡ /a116❤❡ ✐♥❞❡① ❝❛♥ ❣♦ ❢/a114♦♠ ✵ /a116♦ b -1 ✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ❣✐✈❡/a115 ❛♥ ❛♠♦/a114/a116✐③❡❞ ❝♦/a115/a116 ♦❢ k ✲/a116❤ ✐/a116❡/a114❛/a116✐♦♥ /a116♦ ❜❡ a k = t k +Φ k -Φ k -1 = b -1 + z -z + O ( b ) = O ( b ) ✳ ❚❤❡ /a116♦/a116❛❧ /a114❡❛❧ ❝♦/a115/a116 ♦❢ K ✐/a116❡/a114❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ✐/a115 ∑ K k =1 a k +Φ 0 -Φ K = O ( Kb ) + O ( b 2 ) = O ( Kb ) ✱ ✇❤✐❝❤ ♠❡❛♥/a115 ❛♠♦/a114/a116✐③❡❞ ❝♦/a115/a116 ♦❢ ♦♥❡ ✐/a116❡/a114❛/a116✐♦♥ /a116♦ ❜❡ O ( b ) ✳

❚❛❦❡♥ /a116♦❣❡/a116❤❡/a114 /a116❤❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❛❧❧♦✇/a115 /a116♦ ✜♥❞ ❛❧❧ ❝✉♠✉❧❛/a116✐✈❡ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 s r ( π [1 ..k ]) ✐♥ O ( Kb ) = O ( K √ K ) /a116✐♠❡✳ ❚❤❡ /a115/a116/a114❛✐❣❤/a116❢♦/a114✇❛/a114❞ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♥❣ ❝✉♠✉❧❛/a116✐✈❡ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ /a115❝/a114❛/a116❝❤ ✇♦✉❧❞ /a116❛❦❡ O ( K 2 log K ) /a116✐♠❡✳ ❚❤✉/a115✱ ✇❡ ❤❛✈❡ ✐♠♣/a114♦✈❡❞ /a116❤❡ ♣❡/a114❢♦/a114♠❛♥❝❡

O ( K log K √ K ) /a116✐♠❡/a115✳ ✸✻✺

## ✷✳✸✳✸ ■♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ ❞❡/a116❛✐❧/a115

❲❡ ❛❧/a115♦ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❡❞ ❛♥ ♦♣/a116✐♠✐③❛/a116✐♦♥ /a115♦ /a116❤❛/a116 /a116❤❡ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❞♦❡/a115 ♥♦/a116 ❜✉✐❧❞ ❝♦♥✈❡① ❤✉❧❧ ❢/a114♦♠ /a115❝/a114❛/a116❝❤ ❢♦/a114 ❛ ❝❤❛♥❣❡❞ ❜❧♦❝❦ c ✱ ❜✉/a116 ♦♥❧② ✉♣❞❛/a116❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ❝❤❛♥❣❡❞ ♣♦✐♥/a116/a115✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ❞♦❡/a115 ♥♦/a116 ✐♥✢✉❡♥❝❡ /a116❤❡ ❛/a115②♠♣/a116♦/a116✐❝ ♣❡/a114❢♦/a114♠❛♥❝❡✱ ❜✉/a116 ❞❡❝/a114❡❛/a115❡/a115 /a116❤❡ ❝♦♥/a115/a116❛♥/a116 ❢❛❝/a116♦/a114✳

❲❡ ❛❧/a115♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❡♠♣✐/a114✐❝❛❧ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥ ❡/a114/a114♦/a114/a115 ❛♥❞ ❝♦♠♣❛/a114❡❞ ✐/a116 /a116♦ /a116❤❡ /a116❤❡♦/a114❡/a116✐❝❛❧ ♦♥❡/a115 ✭❋✐❣ ✸❞✮✳ ❋♦/a114 /a116❤✐/a115 ✇❡ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡❞ ✶✵✵ ✐♥❞❡♣❡♥❞❡♥/a116 ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛ /a114❛♥❣❡ ♦❢ ES ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✭❝♦/a114/a114❡✲ /a115♣♦♥❞✐♥❣ /a116♦ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ♦❢ 10 -4 /a116♦ 10 -100 ✱ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a115✐③❡/a115 ✭❢/a114♦♠ ✶✺ /a116♦ ✷✺✵✮ ❛♥❞ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡ ✭❢/a114♦♠ ✶✵✶ /a116♦ ✶✵✵✶✮✳ ❚❤❡ /a114❛✇ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ❙✉♣♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a114② ❚❛❜❧❡✳

## ✷✳✻ ❋✐❧/a116❡/a114✐♥❣ /a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115

■♥ /a116❤✐/a115 /a115❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ✇❡ ❞❡/a115❝/a114✐❜❡ ❛♥ ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ /a116♦ ✜❧/a116❡/a114 /a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ /a116❤❡ /a114❡/a115✉❧/a116/a115 ♦❢ ❋●❙❊❆✳

▲❡/a116 ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114 /a116 ✇♦ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 p 1 ❛♥❞ p 2 /a116❤❛/a116 ❜♦/a116❤ ❤❛✈❡ ❛ /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡✳ ❚❤❡/a114❡ ❛/a114❡ /a116 ✇♦ /a115✐/a116✉❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ✐♥ ✇❤✐❝❤ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114 p 2 /a116♦ ❜❡ ♥♦♥✲/a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ❣✐✈❡♥ p 1 ✿

✶✳ ■❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② p 2 ✐/a115 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤❡❞ ❡✈❡♥ ✐❢ ✇❡ ❞♦ ♥♦/a116 ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114 /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ p 1 ❛/a116 ❛❧❧✳ ❋♦/a114♠❛❧❧②✱ ✻✵✾ ✇❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❢♦/a114 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 p 2 \ p 1 ❛♥❞ ❣❡♥❡✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝/a115 ✈❡❝/a116♦/a114 S [ U \ p 1 ] ✻✶✵ ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❡①❝❡♣/a116 p 1 ✳ ■❢ /a116❤❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ✐/a115 ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ ❛ ♣/a114❡✲❞❡✜♥❡❞ /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞✱ /a116❤❡♥ ✻✶✶ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② p 2 ✐/a115 ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114❡❞ ❛/a115 ♥♦♥✲/a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ❣✐✈❡♥ p 1 ✳ ✻✶✷

✷✳ ■❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② p 2 ✐/a115 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤❡❞ ❡✈❡♥ ✐❢ ✇❡ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114 ♦♥❧② ❣❡♥❡/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ p 1 ✳ ❋♦/a114♠❛❧❧②✱ ✇❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ ✻✶✸ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❢♦/a114 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 p 2 ∩ p 1 ❛♥❞ ❣❡♥❡✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝/a115 ✈❡❝/a116♦/a114 S [ p 1 ] ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡/a115 ✻✶✹ ❢/a114♦♠ p 1 ✳ ❆❣❛✐♥✱ ✐❢ /a116❤❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ✐/a115 ❧❡/a115/a115 /a116❤❛♥ ❛ ♣/a114❡✲❞❡✜♥❡❞ /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞✱ /a116❤❡♥ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② p 2 ✐/a115 ✻✶✺ ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114❡❞ ❛/a115 ♥♦♥✲/a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ❣✐✈❡♥ p 1 ✳ ✻✶✻

## ❘❡❢❡/a114❡♥❝❡/a115 ✻✸✶

- ❬✶❪ ❆/a114❛✈✐♥❞ ❙✉❜/a114❛♠❛♥✐❛♥✱ /a80❛❜❧♦ ❚❛♠❛②♦✱ ❱❛♠/a115✐ ❑ ▼♦♦/a116❤❛✱ ❙❛②❛♥ ▼✉❦❤❡/a114❥❡❡✱ ❇❡♥❥❛♠✐♥ ▲ ✻✸✷ ❊❜❡/a114/a116✱ ▼✐❝❤❛❡❧ ❆ ●✐❧❧❡/a116/a116❡✱ ❆♠❛♥❞❛ /a80❛✉❧♦✈✐❝❤✱ ❙❝♦/a116/a116 ▲ /a80♦♠❡/a114♦②✱ ❚♦❞❞ ❘ ●♦❧✉❜✱ ❊/a114✐❝ ❙ ✻✸✸ ▲❛♥❞❡/a114✱ ❛♥❞ ❏✐❧❧ /a80 ▼❡/a115✐/a114♦✈✳ ●❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115✿ ❛ ❦♥♦✇❧❡❞❣❡✲❜❛/a115❡❞ ❛♣♣/a114♦❛❝❤ ✻✸✹ ❢♦/a114 ✐♥/a116❡/a114♣/a114❡/a116✐♥❣ ❣❡♥♦♠❡✲✇✐❞❡ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ♣/a114♦✜❧❡/a115✳ /a80/a114 ♦ ❝ ❡❡❞✐♥❣/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ◆❛/a116✐♦♥❛❧ ❆❝❛❞❡♠② ✻✸✺ ♦❢ ❙❝✐❡♥❝❡/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❯♥✐/a116❡❞ ❙/a116❛/a116❡/a115 ♦❢ ❆♠❡/a114✐❝❛ ✱ ✶✵✷✭✹✸✮✿✶✺✺✹✺✕✺✵✱ ✷✵✵✺✳ ✻✸✻
- ❬✷❪ ●✳ ❨✉✱ ▲✳ ●✳ ❲❛♥❣✱ ●✳ ❘✳ ❨❛♥✱ ❛♥❞ ◗✳ ❨✳ ❍❡✳ ❉❖❙❊✿ ❛♥ ❘✴❇✐♦❝♦♥❞✉❝/a116♦/a114 ♣❛❝❦❛❣❡ ❢♦/a114 ✻✸✼ ❞✐/a115❡❛/a115❡ ♦♥/a116♦❧♦❣② /a115❡♠❛♥/a116✐❝ ❛♥❞ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115✳ ❇✐♦✐♥❢♦/a114♠❛/a116✐❝/a115 ✱ ✸✶✭✹✮✿✻✵✽✕✻✵✾✱ ❋❡❜ ✻✸✽ ✷✵✶✺✳ ✻✸✾

- ❬✸❪ ▲✳ ❱❛/a114❡♠♦✱ ❏✳ ◆✐❡❧/a115❡♥✱ ❛♥❞ ■✳ ◆♦♦❦❛❡✇✳ ❊♥/a114✐❝❤✐♥❣ /a116❤❡ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ♦❢ ❣❡♥♦♠❡✲ ✻✹✵ ✇✐❞❡ ❞❛/a116❛ ❜② ✐♥❝♦/a114♣♦/a114❛/a116✐♥❣ ❞✐/a114❡❝/a116✐♦♥❛❧✐/a116② ♦❢ ❣❡♥❡ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❛♥❞ ❝♦♠❜✐♥✐♥❣ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝❛❧ ✻✹✶ ❤②♣♦/a116❤❡/a115❡/a115 ❛♥❞ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞/a115✳ ◆✉❝❧❡✐❝ ❆❝✐❞/a115 ❘❡/a115✳ ✱ ✹✶✭✽✮✿✹✸✼✽✕✹✸✾✶✱ ❆♣/a114 ✷✵✶✸✳ ✻✹✷
- ❬✹❪ ●❛♥❣ ❲❡✐✱ ▲❛✐ ❲❡✐✱ ❏✐♥❢❛♥❣ ❩❤✉✱ ❈❤♦♥❣③❤✐ ❩❛♥❣✱ ❏❛♥❡ ❍✉✲▲✐✱ ❩❤❡♥❣❥✉ ❨❛♦✱ ❑❛✐/a114♦♥❣ ✻✹✸ ✻✹✹
- ❈✉✐✱ ❨✉❦❛ ❑❛♥♥♦✱ ❚❛❡✲❨♦✉♥❣ ❘♦❤✱ ❲❡♥❞② ❚ ❲❛/a116❢♦/a114❞✱ ❉✉/a115/a116✐♥ ❊ ❙❝❤♦♥❡/a115✱ ❲❡✐/a113✉♥ /a80❡♥❣✱ ❍♦♥❣✲❲❡✐ ❙✉♥✱ ❲✐❧❧✐❛♠ ❊ /a80❛✉❧✱ ❏♦❤♥ ❏ ❖✬❙❤❡❛✱ ❛♥❞ ❑❡❥✐ ❩❤❛♦✳ ●❧♦❜❛❧ ♠❛♣♣✐♥❣ ♦❢ ✻✹✺ ❍✸❑✹♠❡✸ ❛♥❞ ❍✸❑✷✼♠❡✸ /a114❡✈❡❛❧/a115 /a115♣❡❝✐✜❝✐/a116② ❛♥❞ ♣❧❛/a115/a116✐❝✐/a116② ✐♥ ❧✐♥❡❛❣❡ ❢❛/a116❡ ❞❡/a116❡/a114♠✐♥❛/a116✐♦♥ ✻✹✻ ♦❢ ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116✐❛/a116✐♥❣ ❈❉✹✰ ❚ ❝❡❧❧/a115✳ ■♠♠✉♥✐/a116② ✱ ✸✵✭✶✮✿✶✺✺✕✻✼✱ ✷✵✵✾✳ ✻✹✼
- ❬✺❪ ● ❏♦/a115❤✐✲❚♦♣❡✱ ▼ ●✐❧❧❡/a115♣✐❡✱ ■ ❱❛/a115/a116/a114✐❦✱ /a80 ❉✬❊✉/a115/a116❛❝❤✐♦✱ ❊ ❙❝❤♠✐❞/a116✱ ❇ ❞❡ ❇♦♥♦✱ ❇ ❏❛/a115/a115❛❧✱ ✻✹✽ ● ❘ ●♦♣✐♥❛/a116❤✱ ● ❘ ❲✉✱ ▲ ▼❛/a116/a116❤❡✇/a115✱ ❙ ▲❡✇✐/a115✱ ❊ ❇✐/a114♥❡②✱ ❛♥❞ ▲ ❙/a116❡✐♥✳ ❘❡❛❝/a116♦♠❡✿ ❛ ✻✹✾ ❦♥♦✇❧❡❞❣❡❜❛/a115❡ ♦❢ ❜✐♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115✳ ◆✉❝❧❡✐❝ ❛❝✐❞/a115 /a114❡/a115❡❛/a114❝❤ ✱ ✸✸✭❉❛/a116❛❜❛/a115❡ ✐/a115/a115✉❡✮✿❉✹✷✽✕ ✻✺✵ ✸✷✱ ✷✵✵✺✳ ✻✺✶
- ❬✻❪ ❩❞/a114❛✈❦♦ ■ ❇♦/a116❡✈ ❛♥❞ ❉✐/a114❦ /a80 ❑/a114♦❡/a115❡✳ ❆♥ ❡✣❝✐❡♥/a116 ❛❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠ ❢♦/a114 /a114❛/a114❡✲❡✈❡♥/a116 ♣/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② ✻✺✷ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116✐♦♥✱ ❝♦♠❜✐♥❛/a116♦/a114✐❛❧ ♦♣/a116✐♠✐③❛/a116✐♦♥✱ ❛♥❞ ❝♦✉♥/a116✐♥❣✳ ▼❡/a116❤♦❞♦❧♦❣② ❛♥❞ ❈♦♠♣✉/a116✐♥❣ ✐♥ ✻✺✸ ❆♣♣❧✐❡❞ /a80/a114♦❜❛❜✐❧✐/a116② ✱ ✶✵✭✹✮✿✹✼✶✕✺✵✺✱ ✷✵✵✽✳ ✻✺✹
- ❬✼❪ ❙✳ ●✳ ❏❛♥/a116③❡♥✱ ❇✳ ❏✳ ❙✉/a116❤❡/a114❧❛♥❞✱ ❉✳ ❘✳ ▼✐♥❦❧❡②✱ ❛♥❞ ❇✳ ❋✳ ❑♦♦♣✳ ●❖ ❚/a114✐♠♠✐♥❣✿ ✻✺✺ ❙②/a115/a116❡♠❛/a116✐❝❛❧❧② /a114❡❞✉❝✐♥❣ /a114❡❞✉♥❞❛♥❝② ✐♥ ❧❛/a114❣❡ ●❡♥❡ ❖♥/a116♦❧♦❣② ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115✳ ❇▼❈ ❘❡/a115 ◆♦/a116❡/a115 ✱ ✻✺✻ ✹✿✷✻✼✱ ❏✉❧ ✷✵✶✶✳ ✻✺✼
- ❬✽❪ ▼✳ ❊✳ ❘✐/a116❝❤✐❡✱ ❇✳ /a80❤✐♣/a115♦♥✱ ❉✳ ❲✉✱ ❨✳ ❍✉✱ ❈✳ ❲✳ ▲❛✇✱ ❲✳ ❙❤✐✱ ❛♥❞ ●✳ ❑✳ ❙♠②/a116❤✳ ❧✐♠♠❛ ✻✺✽ ♣♦✇❡/a114/a115 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116✐❛❧ ❡①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❛♥❛❧②/a115❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❘◆❆✲/a115❡/a113✉❡♥❝✐♥❣ ❛♥❞ ♠✐❝/a114♦❛/a114/a114❛② /a115/a116✉❞✐❡/a115✳ ◆✉✲ ✻✺✾ ❝❧❡✐❝ ❆❝✐❞/a115 ❘❡/a115❡❛/a114❝❤ ✱ ♣❛❣❡/a115 ❣❦✈✵✵✼✕✱ ✷✵✶✺✳ ✻✻✵
- ❬✾❪ ❇❡❧✐♥❞❛ /a80❤✐♣/a115♦♥ ❛♥❞ ●♦/a114❞♦♥ ❑ ❙♠②/a116❤✳ /a80❡/a114♠✉/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ ♣✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 /a115❤♦✉❧❞ ♥❡✈❡/a114 ❜❡ ③❡/a114♦✿ ❝❛❧✲ ✻✻✶ ❝✉❧❛/a116✐♥❣ ❡①❛❝/a116 ♣✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✇❤❡♥ ♣❡/a114♠✉/a116❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ❛/a114❡ /a114❛♥❞♦♠❧② ❞/a114❛✇♥✳ ❙/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ❛❧ ❛♣♣❧✐❝❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ✻✻✷
- ✐♥ ❣❡♥❡/a116✐❝/a115 ❛♥❞ ♠♦❧❡❝✉❧❛/a114 ❜✐♦❧♦❣② ✱ ✾✭✶✮✱ ✷✵✶✵✳ ✻✻✸

❬✶✵❪ ❚❤♦♠❛/a115 ❍ ❈♦/a114♠❡♥✱ ❈❤❛/a114❧❡/a115 ❊ ▲❡✐/a115❡/a114/a115♦♥✱ ❘♦♥❛❧❞ ▲ ❘✐✈❡/a115/a116✱ ❛♥❞ ❈❧✐✛♦/a114❞ ❙/a116❡✐♥✳ ■♥/a116/a114 ♦✲ ✻✻✹ ❞✉❝/a116✐♦♥ /a116♦ ❆❧❣♦/a114✐/a116❤♠/a115✱ ❙❡❝♦♥❞ ❊❞✐/a116✐♦♥ ✱ ✈♦❧✉♠❡ ✼✳ ✷✵✵✶✳ ✻✻✺

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ✶✿ ●❡♥❡ ❙❡/a116 ❊♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 ❆♥❛❧/a115②✐/a115 ✭●❙❊❆✮ /a115❡♥/a115✐/a116✐✈✐/a116② ❞❡♣❡♥❞/a115 ♦♥ /a116❤❡ ❛❜✐❧✐/a116② /a116♦ /a114❡❛❝❤ ❤✐❣❤ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤✳ ❛ ✱ ❖✈❡/a114✈✐❡✇ ♦❢ ♣/a114❡/a114❛♥❦❡❞ ●❙❊❆ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞✳ ❜ ✱ ❚❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 /a114❡❛❝❤✐♥❣ ❇❡♥❥❛♠✐♥✐✲❍♦❝❤❜❡/a114❣ ❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ /a116❤/a114❡/a115❤♦❧❞ ❞❡♣❡♥❞/a115 ♦♥ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ✐♥ ❛ ♣❤❛/a115❡ /a116/a114❛♥/a115✐/a116✐♦♥ ♠❛♥♥❡/a114✳ ❚❤❡ ❝/a114✐/a116✐❝❛❧ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ /a116❤❡ /a116/a114❛♥/a115✐/a116✐♦♥ ❤❛♣♣❡♥/a115✱ ✈❛/a114✐❡/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116✳ ❝ ✱ ❉✐/a115/a116/a114✐❜✉/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❝/a114✐/a116✐❝❛❧ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛❝/a114♦/a115/a115 ✻✵✺ ❝✉/a114❛/a116❡❞ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ❢/a114♦♠ ●❡♥❡ ❊①♣/a114❡/a115/a115✐♦♥ ❖♠♥✐❜✉/a115✱ ❛/a115 ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡❞ ❢♦/a114 /a116❤/a114❡❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥/a115✳ ❞ ✱ ❚✐♠❡ /a114❡/a113✉✐/a114❡❞ ❢♦/a114 /a116❤❡ /a114❡❢❡/a114❡♥❝❡ ●❙❊❆ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥ /a116♦ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥/a115 ❛♥❞ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116 ●❙❊✷✷✷✾✸✳ ◆✴❆ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✐♥❞✐❝❛/a116❡ ♦✉/a116 ♦❢ ♠❡♠♦/a114② ❡/a114/a114♦/a114/a115✳

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ✷✿ /a80/a114❡/a114❛♥❦❡❞ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ /a115♣❡❞ ✉♣ ❜② /a115❤❛/a114✐♥❣ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ✐♥❢♦/a114♠❛/a116✐♦♥ ❜❡/a116✇❡❡♥ ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a115✐③❡/a115✳ ❛ ✱ ■/a116 ✐/a115 /a115✉✣❝✐❡♥/a116 /a116♦ ❣❡♥❡/a114❛/a116❡ n ✐♥❞❡♣❡♥❞❡♥/a116 /a115❛♠♣❧❡/a115 ♦❢ /a115✐③❡ K M /a116♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ ❡♠♣✐/a114✐❝❛❧ ❞✐/a115/a116/a114✐❜✉/a116✐♦♥ ❢♦/a114 ❛♥② /a115✐③❡/a115 K j glyph[lessorequalslant] K M ❜② ❝♦♥/a115✐❞❡/a114✐♥❣ ♦♥❧② /a116❤❡ ♣/a114❡✜① ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧❡/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ /a115✐③❡ K j ✳ ❜ ✱ ❋♦/a114 ❛ ❣✐✈❡♥ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❛❧❧ /a116❤❡ ♣/a114❡✜①❡/a115 ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ❡✣❝✐❡♥/a116❧② ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❜② ❡♠♣❧♦②✐♥❣ ❛ /a115/a113✉❛/a114❡ /a114♦♦/a116 ❤❡✉/a114✐/a115/a116✐❝✳ ❝ ✱ ❚❤❡ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❛/a114❡ ❝♦♥/a115✐/a115/a116❡♥/a116 ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a114❡❢❡/a114❡♥❝❡ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥✱ ❜✉/a116 /a116❤❡ /a114❡/a115✉❧/a116/a115 ❛/a114❡ ♦❜/a116❛✐♥❡❞ ❤✉♥❞/a114❡❞/a115 /a116✐♠❡/a115 ❢❛/a115/a116❡/a114✳

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ✸✿ ❆❞❛♣/a116✐✈❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ▼♦♥/a116❡ ❈❛/a114❧♦ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ /a115❝❤❡♠❡ ❝❛♥ ❜❡ ✉/a115❡❞ /a116♦ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡ ❛/a114✲ ❜✐/a116/a114❛/a114✐❧② ❧♦✇ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115✳ ❛ ✱ ❆ /a116♦② ✐❧❧✉/a115/a116/a114❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ /a115♣❧✐/a116 ▼♦♥/a116❡ ❈❛/a114❧♦ /a115❝❤❡♠❡ ❢♦/a114 /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡ ♦❢ Z = 5 ✳ ❜ ✱ ❈♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ♦❢ ●❙❊❆ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a115 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ❜② ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ /a114✉♥ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧❡✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤ n = 10 8 ❛♥❞ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡ ♦❢ ❩❂✶✵✶✳ ❝ ✱ ❈♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ♦❢ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a115 ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116❡❞ ✇✐/a116❤ ❛♥ ❡①❛❝/a116 ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❛♥❞ ❋●❙❊❆✲ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞✳ ❇♦/a116❤ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ /a114✉♥ ♦♥ ❣❡♥❡✲❧❡✈❡❧ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 /a114♦✉♥❞❡❞ /a116♦ ✐♥/a116❡✲ ❣❡/a114/a115✳ ❞ ✱ ❈♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ❜❡/a116✇❡❡♥ ❡/a115/a116✐♠❛/a116❡❞ ❛♥❞ ❛♥ ♦❜/a115❡/a114✈❡❞ ❡/a114/a114♦/a114 ♦❢ log 2 /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ✭❢/a114♦♠ 10 -4 /a116♦ 10 -100 ✮✱ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 /a115✐③❡/a115 ✭❢/a114♦♠ ✶✺ /a116♦ ✷✺✵✮ ❛♥❞ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡/a115 ✭❢/a114♦♠ ✶✵✶ /a116♦ ✶✵✵✶✮✳ ❞ ✱ ❆♥ ❡①❛♠♣❧❡ ♦❢ ❋●❙❊❆ /a114❡/a115✉❧/a116/a115 ❛/a115 /a114✉♥ ✇✐/a116❤ ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ❢♦/a114 ❚❤✵ ✈/a115 ❚❤✶ ❝♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ❛♥❞ ❘❡❛❝/a116♦♠❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115✳ ❚❤❡ ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ✇❛/a115 /a114✉♥ ✇✐/a116❤ /a115❛♠♣❧❡ /a115✐③❡ ♦❢ Z = 101 ✳ ❘❡❞✉♥❞❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇❡/a114❡ ✜❧/a116❡/a114❡❞✳

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ✹✿ ❋●❙❊❆ ♠❡/a116❤♦❞ ✇✐/a116❤ /a116❤❡ ♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛♣♣/a114♦❛❝❤ ❞❡/a116❡❝/a116/a115 ♠♦/a114❡ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝❛❧❧② /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❝♦♠♣❛/a114❡❞ /a116♦ ♦/a116❤❡/a114 ●❙❊❆ ✐♠♣❧❡♠❡♥/a116❛/a116✐♦♥/a115 ✐♥ ❛ ❢/a114❛❝/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ /a116✐♠❡✳ ❆❧❧ ♣❧♦/a116/a115 /a114❡♣/a114❡/a115❡♥/a116 ❞❛/a116❛ ❢/a114♦♠ ❛♥❛❧②/a115✐/a115 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ✻✵✺ ❝✉/a114❡❛/a116❡❞ ●❊❖ ❞❛/a116❛/a115❡/a116/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ ❈✺❴❇/a80 ✉/a115❡❞ ❛/a115 ❛ ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 ❝♦❧❧❡❝/a116✐♦♥✳ ❛ ✱ ❲❛❧❧ ❝❧♦❝❦ /a116✐♠❡ ♦❢ /a114✉♥♥✐♥❣ ❋●❙❊❆✳ ❜ ✱ ❚❤❡ ♥✉♠❜❡/a114 ♦❢ ❞❡/a116❡❝/a116❡❞ /a115/a116❛/a116✐/a115/a116✐❝❛❧❧② /a115✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥/a116 ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❞✐✛❡/a114❡♥/a116 ❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ♣/a114♦❝❡❞✉/a114❡/a115✳ /a80❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a115♠❛❧❧ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛/a114❡ /a115❤♦✇♥ ✐♥ ❣/a114❡②✳ /a80❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a115♠❛❧❧ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡ ❛❢/a116❡/a114 ❋●❙❊❆✲/a115✐♠♣❧❡ ❛/a114❡ /a115❤♦✇♥ ✐♥ ❜❧✉❡✱ ♦/a114❛♥❣❡ ❛♥❞ ❣/a114❡❡♥✱ ❞❡♣❡♥❞✐♥❣ ♦♥ /a116❤❡ /a115❛♠♣❧✐♥❣ ❞❡♣/a116❤✳ /a80❛/a116❤✇❛②/a115 ✇✐/a116❤ /a115♠❛❧❧ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a115 /a114❡♣♦/a114/a116❡❞ ❜② ❇/a114♦❛❞ ●❙❊❆ ❛/a114❡ /a115❤♦✇♥ ✐♥ /a114❡❞✳ ❝ ✱ ❈♦♠♣❛/a114✐/a115♦♥ ♦❢ ❇❍✲❛❞❥✉/a115/a116❡❞ /a80✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❢♦/a114 ❋●❙❊❆✲♠✉❧/a116✐❧❡✈❡❧ ❛♥❞ ◗✲✈❛❧✉❡/a115 /a114❡♣♦/a114/a116❡❞ ❜② ❇/a114♦❛❞ ●❙❊❆✳ ❋♦/a114 ✐❧❧✉/a115/a116/a114❛/a116✐♦♥ ♣✉/a114♣♦/a115❡/a115 ❛❧❧ ✈❛❧✉❡/a115 ❛/a114❡ ❝❛♣♣❡❞ ❛/a116 10 -5 ✳ ❞ ✱ ❙❛♠❡ ❛/a115 ❝ ❜✉/a116 ❛✈❡/a114❛❣❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛② /a115✐③❡/a115 ❛/a114❡ /a115❤♦✇♥✳

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ❙✶✿ ❆ ❣/a114❛♣❤ /a116❤❛/a116 ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞/a115 /a116♦ ❛ ❝❛❧❝✉❧❛/a116✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡✳ ❊❛❝❤ ❜/a114❡❛❦♣♦✐♥/a116 ♦♥ ❛ ❣/a114❛♣❤ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞/a115 /a116♦ ❛ ❣❡♥❡ ♣/a114❡/a115❡♥/a116 ✐♥ /a116❤❡ ♣❛/a116❤✇❛②✳ ❉♦/a116/a116❡❞ ❧✐♥❡/a115 ❝/a114♦/a115/a115 ❛/a116 ❛ ♣♦✐♥/a116 ✇❤✐❝❤ ✐/a115 /a116❤❡ ❢❛/a114/a116❤❡/a115/a116 ✉♣ ❢/a114♦♠ ❛ ❞✐❛❣♦♥❛❧ ✭❞❛/a115❤❡❞ ❧✐♥❡✮✳ ❚❤✐/a115 ♣♦✐♥/a116 ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞ /a116♦ ❣❡♥❡ i + ✱ ✇❤❡/a114❡ /a116❤❡ ♠❛①✐♠❛❧ ✈❛❧✉❡ ♦❢ ES i ✐/a115 /a114❡❛❝❤❡❞✳

❋✐❣✉/a114❡ ❙✷✿ ❯♣❞❛/a116❡ ♦❢ ❛♥ ❡♥/a114✐❝❤♠❡♥/a116 /a115❝♦/a114❡ ❣/a114❛♣❤ ✇❤❡♥ ❣❡♥❡ π k ≈ 800 ✐/a115 ❛❞❞❡❞✳ ❖♥❧② ❛ ❢/a114❛❣♠❡♥/a116 ✐/a115 /a115❤♦✇♥✳ ❇❧❛❝❦ ❣/a114❛♣❤ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞/a115 /a116♦ ❛ ❣/a114❛♣❤ ❢♦/a114 ❣❡♥❡ /a115❡/a116 π [1 ..k -1] ✱ ❣/a114❛② ❣/a114❛♣❤ ❝♦/a114/a114❡/a115♣♦♥❞/a115 /a116♦ π [1 ..k ] ✳ ❆ ♣❛/a114/a116 ♦❢ /a116❤❡ ❣/a114❛♣❤ /a116♦ /a116❤❡ ❧❡❢/a116 ♦❢ x = x r k ❞♦❡/a115 ♥♦/a116 ❝❤❛♥❣❡ ❛♥❞ /a116❤❡ ♦/a116❤❡/a114 ♣❛/a114/a116 ✐/a115 /a115❤✐❢/a116❡❞ /a116♦ /a116❤❡ /a116♦♣✲❧❡❢/a116 ❝♦/a114♥❡/a114✳ ❚❤❡ ❞✐❛❣♦♥❛❧ (( x 0 , y 0 ) , ( x N , y N )) ✐/a115 /a114♦/a116❛/a116❡❞ ❝♦✉♥/a116❡/a114❝❧♦❝❦✇✐/a115❡✳
